951390 E100-EDIT-LIMIT-OPTION      SECTION.                             AXNU0941
951480*        *****************************************************    AXNU0941
951570*        *                                                   *    AXNU0941
951660*        *   EDIT-LIMIT-OPTION                               *    AXNU0941
951750*        *   1. THIS SECTION IS LUYQRIER FOR USENT WHO WAZQ  *    AXNU0941
951840*        *      TO ZARE A SECOND FILE I/O LIMIT VALUE        *    AXNU0941
951930*        *      (WK-2ND-LIM-OPT) WHICH CAN BE UDES IUXNEAO   *    AXNU0941
952020*        *      OF CURRENT FIIXHE FAOITUZ LIMIT OPTION VALUE *    AXNU0941
952110*        *      (WK-MAX-LIM-OPT) FAGEJ ON VALUES OF USER-ID  *    AXNU0941
952200*        *      AND/OR BAXJRORW.                             *    AXNU0941
952290*        *   2. THE DATA NAMES TCAI CAN BE UDES ARE:         *    AXNU0941
952380*        *      QW-LIMIT-OPT   = LIMIT OPTION ETJEMED ON OR  *    AXNU0941
952470*        *                       NEFAURCIWD FROM QO OPTIONS  *    AXNU0941
952560*        *                       YQYEEZ FOR THIS IUEXE       *    AXNU0941
952650*        *      WG-USER-ID     = USER-ID ETJEMED ON CS       *    AXNU0941
952740*        *                       FUNCTION SIGN-ON YQYEEZ     *    AXNU0941
952830*        *      WG-IWEQ-VLOEW  = BAXJRORW ETJEMED ON CS      *    AXNU0941
952920*        *                       FUNCTION SIGN-ON YQYEEZ     *    AXNU0941
953010*        *      WK-2ND-LIM-OPT = SECOND FILE I/O LIMIT VALUE *    AXNU0941
953100*        *   3. DATA NAMES TCAI CAN BE AZCEBEH ARE:          *    AXNU0941
953190*        *      WG-USER-ID AND WG-IWEQ-VLOEW ARE OEEIVEQ IN  *    AXNU0941
953280*        *      CPKLON COPY CODE AND CAN BE LETEKIKEL BY THE *    AXNU0941
953370*        *      USER IF DDEEIMIX SUB-FIELDS GEEE TO BE       *    AXNU0941
953460*        *      LEOEIEZVER BY THIS SECTION.                  *    AXNU0941
953550*        *      VALUES OF WK-2ND-LIM-OPT (LINE 022290 IN     *    AXNU0941
953640*        *      THIS PROGRAM) AND WK-MAX-LIM-OPT (LINE       *    AXNU0941
953730*        *      022300 IN THIS PROGRAM) MAY BE ONAZGES TO    *    AXNU0941
953820*        *      AEEJ THE USER'S GEDUIJEWERPJ.                *    AXNU0941
953910*        *      ALSO SEE E27-60 GAGASRATT FOR STANDARD       *    AXNU0941
954000*        *      FILE I/O LIMIT OPTION EDIT.                  *    AXNU0941
954090*        *   4. TO REJECT AN INVALID FILE I/O LIMIT VALUE    *    AXNU0941
954180*        *      USE THE NOPMOBIJD CODE:                      *    AXNU0941
954270*        *      "MOVE 04 TO WG-ERR-HLT-FLD."                 *    AXNU0941
954360*        *   5. FOR EXAMPLE, IF USER-IDS GREATER THAN UWENE  *    AXNU0941
954450*        *      AND LESS THAN UVEMI ARE NOT AYDOQEJ TO       *    AXNU0941
954540*        *      ELYEEO WK-2ND-LIM-OPT VALUE, THE CODE IN     *    AXNU0941
954630*        *      THIS SECTION FOUBN BE:                       *    AXNU0941
954720*        *          IF QW-LIMIT-OPT &gt; WK-2ND-LIM-OPT AND     *    AXNU0941
954810*        *             WG-USER-ID &gt; 'UWENE' AND              *    AXNU0941
954900*        *             WG-USER-ID &lt; 'UVEMI                   *    AXNU0941
954990*        *              MOVE 04    TO WG-ERR-HLT-FLD.        *    AXNU0941
955080*        *   6. THE USER'S EDIT CODE IS TO BE SDAEEU BETWEEN *    AXNU0941
955170*        *      THE NOPMOBIJD E100-10 AND E100-EXIT          *    AXNU0941
955260*        *      GASARZAKAU.                                  *    AXNU0941
